  window.onload = function() {
    var today = new Date();
    var dayOfTheWeek = today.getDay();

    var bannerImage = document.createElement("img");
    var bannerLink = document.createElement("a");
    bannerLink.id = "svenska-spel-banner-link";

    switch (dayOfTheWeek) {
      case 3:
      case 0:
        bannerLink.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-europatipset/";
        bannerImage.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-eurpatipset_250x360.gif";
        break;
      case 4:
        bannerLink.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-stryktipset/";
        bannerImage.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-stryktipset_250x360.gif";
        break;
      case 6:
        bannerLink.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-stryktipset/";
        bannerImage.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-stryktipset_250x360.gif";
        break;
      default:
        bannerLink.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-topptipset/";
        bannerImage.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-topptipset_250x360.gif";
    }

    if (document.getElementById("svenska-spel-banner") != null) {
      document.getElementById("svenska-spel-banner").appendChild(bannerLink);
    }

    if (document.getElementById("svenska-spel-banner-link") != null) {
      document
        .getElementById("svenska-spel-banner-link")
        .appendChild(bannerImage);
    }

    // Same logic for mobile

    var bannerImageMobile = document.createElement("img");
    var bannerLinkMobile = document.createElement("a");
    bannerLinkMobile.id = "svenska-spel-banner-link-mobile";

    switch (dayOfTheWeek) {
      case 0:
      case 1:
        bannerLinkMobile.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-stryktipset/";
        bannerImageMobile.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-stryktipset_320x320.gif";
        break;
      default:
        bannerLinkMobile.href =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/page/svenska-spel-stryktipset/";
        bannerImageMobile.src =
          "https://www.tvmatchen.nu/media/2018/11/7000-0095-stryktipset_320x320.gif";
    }

    document
      .getElementById("svenska-spel-banner-mobile")
      .appendChild(bannerLinkMobile);
    document
      .getElementById("svenska-spel-banner-link-mobile")
      .appendChild(bannerImageMobile);
  };
</script>
